                <span class="description-block" data-ph-id="ph-widget-element-1557952797462-12"> 
                 <ppc-content key="job-it-rich-content-muse-5yEZ79-6IAjK4-ph-paragraph-cc-view1-option1-savedView-1557951570919-savedView-1557946008462-savedView-1557491044466-savedView-1557328613304-savedView-1557146080943-description-text" data-ph-at-id="description-text" class="ppc-text ppc-content" instance-id="6IAjK4" data-ph-id="ph-widget-element-1557952797462-13"> 
                  <h2 style="text-align: center;" data-ph-id="ph-widget-element-1557952797462-14"><span style="line-height:22px;" data-ph-id="ph-widget-element-1557952797462-15"><span style="font-size:18px;" data-ph-id="ph-widget-element-1557952797462-16">Avoid scams. Stay safe in your job search.</span></span></h2> 
                  <div style="text-align: center;" data-ph-id="ph-widget-element-1557952797462-17"> 
                   <span class="ph-line-height-1_3" data-ph-style-attr="ph-line-height-1_3" data-ph-process-line-height="true">Our recruiters only use emails that end in @labcorp.com or @agents.icims.com. Our recruiters will NOT request your personal information (social security number, birth certificate, banking passwords, driver’s license number or passport) and do NOT ask you to make any deposits or purchases. When in doubt, double-check the email address, search the drugdevelopmentcareers.labcorp.com&nbsp;site for our jobs and only apply via our online system. &nbsp;&nbsp;​​​​​​​​​​​​​​</span> 
                  </div> 
                 </ppc-content> </span> 
               </ppc-container> 
              </div> 
             </div> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </section>
